                SELECT 
                    orders.id, 
                    orders.cocktail_id, 
                    cocktails.name AS cocktail_name,
                    users.username, 
                    orders.order_time, 
                    orders.ip_address, 
                    orders.user_agent
                FROM orders
                LEFT JOIN cocktails ON orders.cocktail_id = cocktails.id
                LEFT JOIN users ON orders.user_id = users.id
                ORDER BY orders.order_time DESC

[SQL TRACE]: 
                SELECT 
                    orders.id, 
                    orders.cocktail_id, 
                    cocktails.name AS cocktail_name,
                    users.username, 
                    orders.order_time, 
                    orders.ip_address, 
                    orders.user_agent
                FROM orders
                LEFT JOIN cocktails ON orders.cocktail_id = cocktails.id
                LEFT JOIN users ON orders.user_id = users.id
                ORDER BY orders.order_time DESC

                FROM user_orders
                WHERE DATE(order_time) = DATE('now')

[SQL TRACE]: 
                SELECT 
                    orders.id, 
                    orders.cocktail_id, 
                    cocktails.name AS cocktail_name,
                    users.username, 
                    orders.order_time, 
                    orders.ip_address, 
                    orders.user_agent
                FROM orders
                LEFT JOIN cocktails ON orders.cocktail_id = cocktails.id
                LEFT JOIN users ON orders.user_id = users.id
                ORDER BY orders.order_time DESC
